Abstract: A model of consciousness is proposed which, having a logical basis, lends
itself to simulation using a simple mathematical model called Consciousness as
Entropy Reduction (CER). The approach has been inspired by previous models such
as GWT, IIT and an earlier less mainstream model called "Feature Map" in
Psychology. CER considers the contents of consciousness and subconsciousness as
\textit{scenarios}: a vector of patterns (or features) on various "channels"
(or feature locations). In CER, a feature map itself is not consciousness but
only the input \textit{scenario} into a world of possible subconscious
\textit{scenarios} from which the conscious \textit{scenario} (i.e., conscious
experience) is chosen. Essentially, it creates an internal simulation of the
outside world. Solving problems in simulation internally as a "thought
experiment" is obviously more economical than doing experiments in a real
environment and lends itself to adaptability and hence is a major evolutionary
advantage. CER also has connections with the Hopfield model in artificial
neural networks.

</details>

*P. R. Cabral-Passos,P. S. Azevedo,V. H. Moraes,B. L. Ramalho,A. Duarte,C. D. Vargas*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 研究发现EEG数据可以捕捉随机事件序列的指纹特征，守门员在预测点球序列时，其脑电活动与罚球者序列结构的距离与预测成功率呈负相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证随机事件序列的指纹特征是否可以从行为任务中记录的脑电图数据中提取出来。

Method: 使用守门员游戏，参与者预测概率序列中的每次踢球方向，同时记录EEG活动。通过上下文算法分析EEG片段，计算罚球者序列树与参与者脑电树之间的距离。

Result: 观察到部分电极的距离分布随时间明显减小，表明随着守门员学习序列，EEG依赖关系与罚球者序列树更加一致。距离与守门员成功率成反比。

Abstract: This work draws on the conjecture that fingerprints of stochastic event
sequences can be retrieved from electroencephalographic data (EEG) recorded
during a behavioral task. To test this, we used the Goalkeeper Game
(game.numec.prp.usp.br). Acting as a goalkeeper, the participant predicted each
kick in a probabilistic sequence while EEG activity was recorded. At each
trial, driven by a context tree, the kicker chose one of three options: left,
center, or right. The goalkeeper then predicted the next kick by pressing a
button. Tree estimation was performed by applying the Context Algorithm to EEG
segments locked to the button press (-300 to 0 ms). We calculated the distance
between the penalty taker's tree and the trees retrieved per participant and
electrode. This metric was then correlated with the goalkeeper's success rates.
We observed a clear reduction in the overall distance distribution over time
for a subset of electrodes, indicating that EEG dependencies become more
congruent with the penalty taker's tree as the goalkeeper learns the sequence.
This distance is inversely proportional to the goalkeepers' success rates,
indicating a clear relationship between performance and the neural signatures
associated with the sequence structure.

</details>

*Ahsan J. Cheema,Sunil Puria*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 隐性听力损失（耳蜗神经变性）会破坏超阈值听觉编码但不影响临床阈值，难以诊断。需要找到能有效揭示这种神经退化的语音刺激。

Method: 使用现象学听觉模型模拟50个CVC单词在不同条件下的响应，包括清晰、时间压缩、混响和组合条件，在不同呈现水平和不同自发放电率纤维存活率下计算内毛细胞与听神经纤维响应之间的互信息。

Conclusion: 快速、时间密集的语音是检测隐性听力损失的最佳探针，这为设计客观临床诊断工具提供了依据，同时揭示了使用混响作为探针的局限性。

Abstract: Hidden hearing loss, or cochlear neural degeneration (CND), disrupts
suprathreshold auditory coding without affecting clinical thresholds, making it
difficult to diagnose. We present an information-theoretic framework to
evaluate speech stimuli that maximally reveal CND by quantifying mutual
information (MI) loss between inner hair cell (IHC) receptor potentials and
auditory nerve fiber (ANF) responses and acoustic input and ANF responses.
Using a phenomenological auditory model, we simulated responses to 50 CVC words
under clean, time-compressed, reverberant, and combined conditions across
different presentation levels, with systematically varied survival of low-,
medium-, and high-spontaneous-rate fibers. MI was computed channel-wise between
IHC and ANF responses and integrated across characteristic frequencies.
Information loss was defined relative to a normal-hearing baseline. Results
demonstrate progressive MI loss with increasing CND, most pronounced for
time-compressed speech, while reverberation produced comparatively smaller
effects. These findings identify rapid, temporally dense speech as optimal
probes for CND, informing the design of objective clinical diagnostics while
revealing problems associated with reverberation as a probe.

beamforming.

### [209] [Two-scale branching functions and inhomogeneous attractors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.07013)
*Vilma Orgoványi,Alex Rutar*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文引入了任意度量空间的两尺度分支函数概念，该函数编码了下盒维数、上盒维数和Assouad谱。对于准加倍度量空间，该函数近似Lipschitz连续。作者完全分类了可实现的Lipschitz两尺度分支函数，并研究了满足标准分离条件的非齐次自共形集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究度量空间的分形维数特性，特别是开发能够统一描述多种维数概念（下盒维数、上盒维数、Assouad谱）的数学工具，并应用于非齐次自共形集的分析。

Method: 引入两尺度分支函数概念，证明其在准加倍度量空间中的Lipschitz性质，完全分类可实现的Lipschitz两尺度分支函数。然后研究非齐次自共形集，建立吸引子的两尺度分支函数与凝聚集两尺度分支函数及齐次吸引子Hausdorff维数的显式关系。

Result: 获得了两尺度分支函数的完整分类，给出了非齐次自共形吸引子的下盒维数和Assouad谱的显式公式，这些公式通过凝聚集的两尺度分支函数和齐次吸引子的Hausdorff维数表达。

Conclusion: 两尺度分支函数为分析度量空间的维数特性提供了统一框架，在非齐次自共形集的情况下能够给出维数的显式计算，扩展了分形几何的理论工具和应用范围。

Abstract: We introduce the notion of a two-scale branching function associated with an
arbitrary metric space, which encodes the lower and upper box dimensions as
well as the Assouad spectrum. If the metric space is quasi-doubling, this
function is approximately Lipschitz. We fully classify the attainable Lipschitz
two-scale branching functions, which gives a new proof of the classification of
Assouad spectra due to the second author.
  We then study inhomogeneous self-conformal sets satisfying standard
separation conditions. We show that the two-scale branching function of the
attractor is given explicitly in terms of the two-scale branching function of
the condensation set and the Hausdorff dimension of the homogeneous attractor.
In particular, this gives formulas for the lower box dimension and the Assouad
spectrum of the attractor.

</details>


### [210] [Functional Equations for Generalized Collatz Dynamics Using Integral Representations and Residue Calculus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.06736)
*Christos N. Efrem*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文系统推导了Collatz型算术动力学中生成函数的递归公式和函数方程，主要使用复分析工具如围道积分、留数计算和柯西积分公式，并推广到多维情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Collatz型算术动力学的生成函数性质，建立系统化的分析方法，推广Egorychev方法到更广泛的应用领域。

Method: 使用复分析工具（围道积分、留数计算、柯西积分公式），基于Egorychev方法，并扩展到多维复变函数。

Result: 成功推导出生成函数的递归公式和函数方程，将方法推广到多维情形，建立了系统化的分析框架。

Conclusion: 该方法为Collatz型算术动力学提供了有效的分析工具，扩展了Egorychev方法的应用范围，为相关研究建立了理论基础。

Abstract: This paper focuses on a wide class of Collatz-type arithmetic dynamics, and
presents a systematic derivation of recursive formulas and functional equations
satisfied by the associated generating functions. The main tools belong to
complex analysis, including contour-integral representations, residue calculus,
and Cauchy's integral formulas. The basic approach is inspired by Egorychev's
method, which has been used so far to establish combinatorial identities.
Moreover, this work generalizes existing results and extends the methodology to
multiple dimensions using several complex variables.

</details>


### [211] [Disconnected large bifurcation supports and Cartesian products of bifurcations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.07036)
*Timur Bakiev,Yulij S. Ilyashenko*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 该论文证明了当大分岔支撑集不连通且在每个连通分量的邻域上原族结构稳定时，分岔族可以分解为各分量附近分岔的笛卡尔积。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究多参数分岔族何时可以分解为独立分岔的笛卡尔积，以简化分岔分析。

Method: 通过分析大分岔支撑集的连通性，并在每个连通分量的邻域上要求结构稳定性来证明分解定理。

Result: 证明了当大分岔支撑集不连通且满足结构稳定性条件时，分岔族确实可以分解为笛卡尔积。

Conclusion: 结构稳定性条件对于分岔族的笛卡尔积分解是必要的，不能省略。

Abstract: A bifurcation that occurs in a multiparameter family is a Cartesian product
if it splits into two factors in the sense that one bifurcation takes place in
one part of the phase portrait, another one -- in another part, and they are in
a sense independent, do not interact with each other. To understand how a
family bifurcates, it is sufficient to study it in a neighborhood of the
so-called large bifurcation support. Given a family of vector fields on $S^2$
that unfolds a field $v_0$, the respective large bifurcation support is a
closed $v_0$-invariant subset of the sphere indicating parts of the phase
portrait of $v_0$ affected by bifurcations. One should consider disconnected
large bifurcation supports in order to obtain Cartesian products for sure. We
prove that, if the large bifurcation support is disconnected and the
restriction of the original family to some neighborhood of each connected
component is structurally stable (plus some mild extra conditions), then the
original family is a Cartesian product of the bifurcations that occur near the
components of the large bifurcation support. We also show that the structural
stability requirement cannot be omitted.

</details>


### [212] [Two irrationally elliptic closed orbits of Reeb flows on the boundary of star-shaped domain in $\mathbb{R}^{2n}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.06597)
*Xiaorui Li,Hui Liu,Wei Wang*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 该论文证明在具有恰好n个素闭轨道的动态凸Reeb流中，至少有两个轨道是无限椭圆型的


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决哈密顿动力学中关于星形域边界上Reeb流的两个长期猜想：一个是关于闭轨道数量的猜想，另一个是关于凸域中闭轨道椭圆性质的猜想

Method: 研究星形域边界上的动态凸Reeb流，分析具有恰好n个素闭轨道的情况

Result: 证明了当存在恰好n个素闭轨道时，其中至少两个必须是无限椭圆型的

Conclusion: 这一结果为两个长期存在的猜想提供了部分支持，特别是在动态凸Reeb流的情况下

Abstract: There are two long-standing conjectures in Hamiltonian dynamics concerning
Reeb flows on the boundaries of star-shaped domains in $\mathbb{R}^{2n}$ ($n
\geq 2$). One conjecture states that such a Reeb flow possesses either $n$ or
infinitely many prime closed orbits; the other states that all the closed Reeb
orbits are irrationally elliptic when the domain is convex and the flow
possesses finitely many prime closed orbits. In this paper, we prove that for
dynamically convex Reeb flow on the boundary of a star-shaped domain in
$\mathbb{R}^{2n}$ ($n \geq 2$) with exactly $n$ prime closed orbits, at least
two of them must be irrationally elliptic.

</details>


### [213] [Local well-posedness for a class of semilinear Moore-Gibson-Thompson equations with subcritical nonlinearities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.06944)
*Flank D. M. Bezerra,Luís M. Salge*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文研究了受Dell'Oro、Liverani和Pata(2023)提出的Moore-Gibson-Thompson模型启发的高阶半线性发展方程，涉及具有齐次边界条件的强椭圆算子。证明了在亚临界非线性条件下相应半线性柯西问题的局部适定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高阶半线性发展方程的适定性问题，特别是处理算子缺乏增生性和有界虚幂性质的情况，阐明外推空间和分数阶域在处理这些问题中的作用。

Method: 利用算子的扇形性质和零属于预解集的特点，构建分数幂空间并分析其谱性质，通过外推空间和分数阶域的方法处理算子缺乏增生性的问题。

Result: 证明了在亚临界非线性条件下，相应半线性柯西问题的局部适定性。

Conclusion: 该框架阐明了外推空间和分数阶域在处理算子缺乏增生性和有界虚幂性质问题中的关键作用，为类似高阶发展方程的研究提供了有效方法。

Abstract: In this paper, we study a class of higher-order semilinear evolution
equations inspired by the Moore-Gibson-Thompson model introduced by Dell'Oro,
Liverani and Pata (2023), involving strongly elliptic operators of order ($2m$)
with homogeneous boundary conditions. The associated unbounded linear operator
is a sectorial operator with zero belonging to the resolvent set, allowing the
construction of fractional powers spaces, and the analysis of their spectral
properties. We prove the local well-posedness of the corresponding semilinear
Cauchy problem under subcritical nonlinearities. Our framework clarifies the
role of extrapolation spaces and fractional domains in handling the lack of
accretivity and bounded imaginary powers of the operator.

</details>

### [214] [Reversible computations are computations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.06585)
*Clément Aubert,Jean Krivine*

Main category: cs.LO

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一个因果模型的保守扩展，用于容纳可逆计算，通过在配置结构中引入对称剩余操作，并证明稳定配置结构在此操作下保持稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 因果关系作为并发系统的抽象时间概念，但现有模型未考虑可逆事件的情况，需要扩展因果模型以支持可逆计算。

Method: 在配置结构模型中引入对称剩余操作来建模可逆计算，证明稳定配置结构在此操作下保持稳定，并为素数事件结构推导可逆计算语义。

Result: 建立了可逆计算的因果模型，证明稳定配置结构在对称剩余操作下保持稳定，并显示可逆计算语义与交换操作（对偶化冲突和因果关系）一致。

Conclusion: 简单因果关系要求同样适用于可逆事件，提出的扩展模型成功地将因果概念应用于可逆计算场景。

Abstract: Causality serves as an abstract notion of time for concurrent systems. A
computation is causal, or simply valid, if each observation of a computation
event is preceded by the observation of its causes. The present work
establishes that this simple requirement is equally relevant when the
occurrence of an event is invertible. We propose a conservative extension of
causal models for concurrency that accommodates reversible computations. We
first model reversible computations using a symmetric residuation operation in
the general model of configuration structures. We show that stable
configuration structures, which correspond to prime algebraic domains, remain
stable under the action of this residuation. We then derive a semantics of
reversible computations for prime event structures, which is shown to coincide
with a switch operation that dualizes conflict and causality.

</details>
